\DoxyCodeLine{00773\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ N\ =\ ceil\ (\ pi\ /\ acos(1\ -\/\ error\ /\ r)\ )\ \ \ \ \ where\ r\ >\ 0,\ error\ <=\ r}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00776\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ will\ get\ this\ result.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00777\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00778\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Rendering\ circles\ with\ an\ odd\ number\ of\ segments,\ while\ mathematically\ correct\ will\ produce}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00779\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ asymmetrical\ results\ on\ the\ raster\ grid.\ Therefore\ we're\ rounding\ N\ to\ next\ even\ number\ (7-\/>8,\ 8-\/>8,\ 9-\/>10\ etc.)}}
